 is sanshodhan ke jariye sarkaar ne 2 meter tak kii khudaai ko khanan kii shrenee se baahar kar diya
 The condition was that the machine should not be used
 8 maheene pehle ye sanshodhan kiya gaya tha

 The Chief Minister said that a proposal for the construction of new police stations should be prepared and sent to the Government of India
 kendra sarkaar ke sahyog se thana nirmaan kii yojana ko punerjeevit kiya jaae
 He also said that the police recruitment process should be discriminatory and corruption free

 is kaaran bhartiyon prabhavit hoti hai or vilamb hota he

 uttar pradesh ek bada rajya he or sansadhano kii kami bhi he kintu police apni kaary pranali or charitra se aisa parivartan laae, jisase aam janata kii pidaa kaa nivaaran ho sake
 He said, "it is our moral responsibility to provide security to every person of the state
 suraksha or shaanti ke liye khatra paidaa karne vaale logon ko chihnit kar karrwai kii jaae

 ’’ Yogi said that provision of public amenities should be made in the police stations and there should be friendly treatment with the public

 Khan, who has assumed charge of the Ministry of Minority Affairs, said that although reservation is not the solution to all problems, it is true for those who are backward or have been victims of discrimination
 musalamaanon ke liye 4
 Unaffected by the adverse judgment of the court on the 5% sub quota, Khan feels that the order came due to some flaws from the government and it does not actually reject the sub quota proposal

 5 fisadi up kota ke bare main) kuch takneekee khamiyaan thim jinaki ore supreme court or andhrapradesh hai court ke faislon main sanket kiya gaya

 lekin vah maanate hai ki aarakshan ek adhikaar he

 ’ unhone kaha, ‘iske antargat sarkaar samuchit vyavastha kar sakati he

 ’ dalit isaayiyon or dalit musalamaanon ko aarakshan dene ke jatil mudde par khan ne kaha ki vah koshish karenge ki aisa ho jaae
